***ster.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ster.html>ster</a> (1532)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:sterre.html>sterre</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sterne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sterro</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sterno</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sternô</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sternǭ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂stḗr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ster.html>ster</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sterren.html>sterren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sterretje.html>sterretje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>star</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> otherwise  archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> any luminous astronomical or meteorological phenomenon</li>
<li>star <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">person</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ol><li>one who excels in something</li>
<li>celebrity</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">television</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> short advertisement</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sterk.html>sterk</a> (825)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">starc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sterc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:stark.html>stark</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*starkaz</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>strong, having physical strength</li>
<li>concentrated, strong, powerful in taste</li>
<li>implausible, improbable</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Germanic  grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> strong, pertaining to strong nouns, strong declension</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sterkte.html>sterkte</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>Expression used to wish someone the strength to persevere whatever hardship they are experiencing</li>
<li>"<span class="Latn" lang="en">good luck</span>"</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sterkte.html>sterkte</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sterkten.html>sterkten</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sterktes.html>sterktes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>strength of materials or of optic devices such as lenses of mirrors.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:sterven.html>sterven</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stervan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sterbaną</i>, itself either from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)terp-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lose force; lose sensibility, become numb; be dead, be motionless</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sterbʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be stiff, become stiff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>support</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> backup</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:dolen.html>dole</a>, unemployment benefit</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:steunen.html>steunen</a> (2985)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stōnen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stunōn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stonōn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*stunōn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stunōną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to groan</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)tenh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to thunder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stun</i>.
</p>

</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to moan, groan</li></ol>

***steur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:steur.html>steur</a> (53153)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">store</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sturo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sturjô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sturgeon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also Old High German <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">sturio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sturgeon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">styria</i>; from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sturjô</i>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">осётр</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osjótr</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sturgeon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">eršketras</i>; of obscure origin, but possibly related to the root of <span class="Latn" lang="en">stir</span>. Other <a href = vnd.unilang:theories.html>theories</a> trace it to a <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> Pre-Indo European language of Scandinavia.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">sturgeon</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:steven.html>steven</a> (3802)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stēvene</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>the part of a ship's <span class="Latn" lang="en">deck</span> that stretches along the entire length of the <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:keel.html>keel</a></span> including the <span class="Latn" lang="en">bow</span> and the <span class="Latn" lang="en">stern</span></li></ol>

<p><b>steward</b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>

***stiekum.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stiekum.html>stiekum</a> (72697)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stiekem.html>stiekem</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:stiekum.html>stiekum</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">regional<span class="ib-comma">,</span> north-western Germany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> discreetly, secretly
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:das.html>Das</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mach.html>mach</a> ich <a href = vnd.unilang:ganz.html>ganz</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stiekum.html>stiekum</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:das.html>Das</a> kriegt keiner mit.</i>
<dl><dd>I do that quite <b>discreetly</b>. Nobody will know.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> common chiefly in the western <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> of Westphalia. In adjacent regions it also widely understood, but not often <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a>.
</p>
</body> 
***stiel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stiel.html>stiel</a> (62870)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stiel.html>stiel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">estile</i>. Doublet with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stijl.html>stijl</a></i>.
</p>

***stig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stig.html>stig</a> (29616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stīgō</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stīganą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">climb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> ( gt; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">stīgan</i>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stige</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">stiga</i>. A masculine Germanic variant <i>*stīgaz</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> indicated by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">stic</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:steig.html>Steig</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">stígr</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:stig.html>stig</a></i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang">stīġ</strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latinx" lang="ang">stīġa</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latinx" lang="ang">stīġe</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>path (especially steep or narrow)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stiją</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">stí</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">sti</i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang">stiġ</strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latinx" lang="ang"><strong class="selflink">stiġ</strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hall, building, sty</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stijgen.html>stijgen</a> (5248)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stigen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stīgan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stīganą</i>.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ascend</li></ol>

***stikken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stikken.html>stikken</a> (5343)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sticken</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stikken.html>stikken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to choke, suffocate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suffocate, to cause problems with breathing</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to teem [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a></i> <span>(with)</span></span>] <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to have an abundance of</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

***stilleven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stilleven.html>stilleven</a> (50623)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stil.html>stil</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">still, motionless, silent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">life</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, perhaps from older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stilstaand.html>stilstaand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stilleven.html>stilleven</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stillevens.html>stillevens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stilleven.html>stilleventje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">still-life</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">painting or other image of arranged inanimate or dead <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a>, sometimes displaying living animals as well</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from late 17th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1678</b>, Samuel <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Hoogstraeten, <i>Inleyding <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Hooge Schoole <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Schilderkonst: <a href = vnd.unilang:anders.html>Anders</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Zichtbaere Werelt</i>, publ. by Fransois <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Hoogstraeten, page 87.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:echter.html>Echter</a> ſtaet <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> vaſt, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> overaerdig eenige <a href = vnd.unilang:bloemen.html>bloemen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vruchten.html>vruchten</a>, of <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <b>ſtillevens</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijk</a> wy'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noemen.html>noemen</a>, geſchildert <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>, deeze Schilderyen <a href = vnd.unilang:evenwel.html>evenwel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> hooger, <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> in den eerſten graed <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> konſtwerken moogen geſtelt <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> waerenze <a href = vnd.unilang:zelfs.html>zelfs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Heem</i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:pater.html>Pater</a> Zegers</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:jae.html>jae</a> Zeuxis <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Parraſius, <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> bedriegens <a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a> uitgevoert.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">However, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> certain, that no matter how exceedingly charming some flowers, fruits or other <b>still <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a></b>, as <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> call it, have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> painted, these paintings may nevertheless not be placed any <a href = vnd.unilang:higher.html>higher</a> than in the first [lowest] degree of artworks; <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> if they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> executed to the point of deceptive realism by <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Heem, father Zegers, <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> Zeuxis and Parrhasius.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:stilleven.html>stilleven</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:artistieke.html>artistieke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:compositie.html>compositie</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:schilderij.html>schilderij</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:tekening.html>tekening</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:foto.html>foto</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roerloos.html>roerloze</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:levenloos.html>levenloze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:objecten.html>objecten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zorg.html>zorg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:belicht.html>belicht</a>
